### direct-extension-market-parse-request

- Category: `direct`
- Verb: `extensions.market.parse_request`
- HTTP status: `200`
- Request OK: `True`
- Functional OK: `True`
- Duration: `1 ms`
- Request payload:
```json
{
  "cap_version": "0.2.2",
  "params": {
    "request": {
      "cap_version": "0.2.2",
      "params": {
        "node_id": "demand",
        "scope": "parents"
      },
      "verb": "graph.neighbors"
    }
  },
  "request_id": "direct-extension-market-parse-request-1776819976725",
  "verb": "extensions.market.parse_request"
}
```
- Response:
```json
{

  "request_id": "direct-extension-market-parse-request-1776819976725",

    "effective_options": {
      "debug": {
        "include_runtime_config": false
      },
      "graph_operations": {
        "local_graph": {
          "max_hops": 1,
          "max_nodes": 64
        }
      }
    },

      "input_requirements": [
        "params.node_id",
        "params.scope"
      ],
      "primary_functions": [
        {
          "function": "neighbors",
          "module": "example_cap_server.toy_graph",
          "purpose": "Return immediate parents or children of node."
        }
      ],

      "node_ids": [
        "demand"
      ],
      "params": {
        "node_id": "demand",

}
```

### pipeline-extensions-example-scenario_compare

- Category: `pipeline`
- Verb: `extensions.market.interpret_request`
- HTTP status: `200`
- Request OK: `True`
- Functional OK: `True`
- Duration: `1 ms`
- Pipeline stages: `{"analysis": "success", "calculation": "success", "graph_operations": "success", "parse": "success", "postprocess": "success"}`
- Request payload:

### pipeline-extensions-example-intervention_battle

- Category: `pipeline`
- Verb: `extensions.market.interpret_request`
- HTTP status: `200`
- Request OK: `True`
- Functional OK: `True`
- Duration: `1 ms`
- Pipeline stages: `{"analysis": "success", "calculation": "success", "graph_operations": "success", "parse": "success", "postprocess": "success"}`

```json
  "params": {

      "params": {
        "disruption_penalty": 1.0,
        "min_effect_threshold": 0.0001,
        "outcome_node": "revenue",
        "plan_a": {
          "interventions": [
            {
              "intervention_delta": 1.5,
              "target_node": "marketing_spend"
            }
          ],
          "name": "acquisition_heavy"
        },
        "plan_b": {
          "interventions": [
            {
              "intervention_delta": 1.0,
              "target_node": "product_quality"
            }
          ],
          "name": "product_heavy"
        }
      },
      "verb": "extensions.example.intervention_battle"
    }
  },
```
